LxcgTM (mm)
Full Name: Lx distance to inst. CG, unit 1
Type: Lx distance (local -X coord.)
Legend: Instant CG, total mass, unit 1
Component: Chassis motion
More details: This is the local X coordinate of the instant CG of the vehicle unit in the sprung mass coordinate system, with the sign flipped as needed to represent the distance behind the sprung-mass origin. Be aware that the motion of the instant CG cannot be measured directly in physical vehicles.

ModeTran (-)
Full Name: Transmission control mode
Type: Transmission control mode
Legend: Transmission control mode
Component: Powertrain
More details: Control option for transmission, from configurable function MODE_TRANS or imported variable. -1 is reverse, 0 is neutral, 1 specifies open-loop mode, 2 and higher specify a closed-loop limit (maximum gear available to the controller). The current gear in closed-loop mode is Gear_CL. The current gear in open-loop mode is Gear_OL.

target_offset (-)
8-Char Alias: trgtOfft
Full Name: target_offset
Type: target_offset
Legend: target_offset
Component: VS Commands

TC_Lock (-)
Full Name: Torque converter lockup signal
Type: Boolean
Legend: Torque converter lockup clutch
Component: Powertrain
More details: Torque converter lockup clutch control signal: 0 -> free, 1 -> lockup.

Throttle (-)
Full Name: Normalized throttle at Pedal
Type: Dimensionless ratio
Legend: Pedal
Component: Powertrain
More details: Sum of the specified open-loop throttle control (internal + imported) plus throttle due to closed-loop speed control.

Thrtl_SC (-)
Full Name: Throttle (speed controller)
Type: Dimensionless ratio
Legend: Pedal (speed controller)
Component: Powertrain

Thr_Eng (-)
Full Name: Normalized throttle at Engine
Type: Dimensionless ratio
Legend: Engine
Component: Powertrain
More details: Normalized throttle applied to the engine. This includes a 1st-order time lag.

Thr_Intl (-)
Full Name: Normalized throttle (internal)
Type: Dimensionless ratio
Legend: Pedal (internal)
Component: Powertrain
More details: Sum of the specified open-loop throttle control plus throttle due to closed-loop speed control. This excludes the optional imported value.

T_Event (s)
Full Name: Time since event clock reset
Type: Time
Legend: Event
Component: Time
More details: This output is calculated each time step with the formula T_EVENT = T - TSTART_T_EVENT, where TSTART_T_EVENT is a system parameter that may be set to T when a VS Event is triggered.

T_Record (s)
Full Name: Recording time in output file
Type: Time
Legend: Recording time in file
Component: Time
More details: This variable is incremented when outputs are written to file or saved to a buffer. This matches the time that is obtained in post-processing by multiplying the sample number by the sample interval.

More details: Equivalent wheel speed is defined as the spin (rad/sec) multiplied by the effective rolling radius. It is the translational speed that corresponds to the angular rate during free rolling.
